Player A: you are going to place the following ships. For each ship, type the coordinate of the upper left side of the ship, followed by either H (for horizontal) or V (for vertical) or U (for up direction) or D (for down direction) or L (for left direction) or R (for right direction). For example M4H would place a ship horizontally starting at M4 and going to the right. You have

2 'Submarine' ships that are 1x2
3 'Destroyers' that are 1x3
3 'Battleships' that are 'T' shaped
2 'Carriers' that are 'Z' shaped
